This is a function of A only (no t dependence). It has a linear term in A and a sin(A) term.

**Key observations about GT:**
1. No t dependence
2. Contains sin(c*A) — a sinusoidal term in A
3. Contains a linear term in A
4. No constant offset (when A=0, GT = 0)

**Candidates with sin() involving A:**

**Candidate 7:** `A**3*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(A*c5 + c6))`
This has exp(sin(...)), not sin(...). Can't match.

**Candidate 19:** `A**3*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + c3*tanh(c4*t + c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`
Set c0=0, c1=0 to remove cubic and quadratic. Set c3=0 to remove tanh. Then: `A*c2 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`. The sin argument is `c7*log(c8*A + 1)`, not linear in A. For small c8*A, log(1+c8*A) ≈ c8*A, but this is only approximate, not exact. **No match.**

Similar issue — sin of log, not sin of A. **No match.**

**Candidate 50:** `A*c0 + c1*tanh(c2*t + c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7) + c8*log(A**3*c9 + 1)`
Again sin(log(...)), not sin(A). **No match.**

**Candidate 37:** `A**c0*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6/(c7 + t))`
Set c4=0, c6=0: `c1*A**c0 + c3*A**c2 + c5`. This gives power-law terms, no sin. **No match.**

Going through all 50 candidates, the only ones with `sin` are: 7 (inside exp), 19 (of log), 30 (of log), 50 (of log). None have `sin(c*A)` directly.

Can sin(c*A) be represented by other functions? No — sin is transcendental and cannot be exactly represented by polynomials, exponentials, logs, tanh, or their combinations over all A.

Could any candidate with enough polynomial terms approximate? No — polynomial approximation is never exact equivalence.

**Candidate 35:** `A**3*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*log(A*c4 + c5*t + 1) + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)`
The term `c6*log(c7*exp(c8*A) + 1)` — for large c8*A this is approximately c6*c8*A + c6*log(c7), for small c8*A it behaves differently. This cannot produce sin(A). **No match.**
